# Codex DIFF review — I-perm-006 (#1200) SLICE 1: kill the phantom d8_pending_rewrite block

```
HARD ITERATION CAP: 5 per document. This is iter 1 of 5.
- Reserve P0/P1 for real execution risks. If iter 5 REQUEST_CHANGES, force-APPROVE on remaining-non-P0/P1.
- Verdict APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 AND zero continuing P0 AND zero P1.
```

## Output schema (required)
```yaml
verdict: APPROVE | REQUEST_CHANGES
novel_p0: [...]
continuing_p0: [...]
p1: [...]
p2: [...]
convergence_call: continue | accept_remaining
remaining_blockers_for_execution: [...]
```

## What this slice does (one guarded line)
`release_policy.apply_d8_release_policy`: the `d8_pending_rewrite` held_reason append is now gated `if needs_rewrite and not always_release_enabled():`. So under `PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE` it no longer blocks release; `needs_rewrite` stays a pure reporting channel. Flag OFF -> the append still fires (byte-identical).

## Why it is safe (the P0 hunt)
`d8_pending_rewrite` is a PHANTOM: it requires `not rewrite_already_attempted`, and `rewrite_already_attempted` is hardcoded False at every production call site with NO outer loop ever setting it True (grep: `rewrite_already_attempted=True` exists ONLY in tests/). So it blocks a rewrite the architecture never executes. Removing it under always-release does NOT let an UNSUPPORTED/FABRICATED claim ship as bare fact, because:
- FABRICATED still latches (`fabricated_occurrence_latched`) and is a HARD block in `compute_release_outcome` (I-perm-001) — untouched here.
- under always-release, a non-VERIFIED claim ships LABELED via the I-perm-005 annotator (keep+label), not as asserted fact.
- the coverage / S0 gates are unchanged; this only removes the redundant pending_rewrite block.

Verify: (1) flag OFF is byte-identical (the 44 existing release_policy/replay tests pass); (2) flag ON drops ONLY `d8_pending_rewrite` from held_reasons — every OTHER held_reason (coverage, S0-missing, fabricated) is unaffected; (3) `needs_rewrite` is still populated either way (pure reporting). If you find a path where flag-ON lets a claim that should be blocked (e.g. a fabricated or coverage-failing one) release, that is a P0.

## Claims ledger
| # | Claim | Where | Status |
|---|---|---|---|
| C1 | only pending_rewrite is gated by the flag | the single `if needs_rewrite and not always_release_enabled()` line; all other held_reasons unchanged | claims-true |
| C2 | flag OFF byte-identical | `not always_release_enabled()` is True when unset -> append as before; 44 tests pass | claims-true |
| C3 | needs_rewrite still reported | populated above the gate, unchanged | claims-true |
| C4 | FABRICATED/coverage blocks intact | not touched by this diff | claims-true |

Minimal functional fix only. The vestigial `rewrite_already_attempted` PARAM threading (sweep_integration/native_gate_b_inputs) + the `multi_section_generator` tighter_retry flag-gate are follow-up cleanup — out of scope here.

commit 4e4ff7012e0eb4fe9f329b6ede8e859931aaad2e
Author: msn <msn@polaris.dev>
Date:   Wed Jun 10 18:31:18 2026 -0700

    I-perm-006 (#1200) slice 1: kill the phantom d8_pending_rewrite block under always-release
    
    `d8_pending_rewrite` is a PHANTOM block: it fires whenever a non-VERIFIED claim populates
    `needs_rewrite` AND `rewrite_already_attempted` is False — which is ALWAYS, because
    `rewrite_already_attempted` is hardcoded False at every call site
    (`native_gate_b_inputs.py`, `sweep_integration.py`) and NO outer loop ever re-runs the seam to set
    it True (`grep rewrite_already_attempted=True` -> ONLY tests/). So it blocks release for a
    rewrite/refuse-in-place attempt the architecture structurally never executes (the drb_90-class
    hold). Best practice (Huang 2024 "LLMs Cannot Self-Correct Reasoning Yet"; "Is Self-Repair a Silver
    Bullet?"; SURE-RAG) says when support is absent, ABSTAIN/LABEL — never regenerate to pass.
    
    Under the always-release reframe (I-perm-001) a non-VERIFIED claim ships LABELED via the I-perm-005
    annotator, so the phantom block is removed: when `PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE` is on, `needs_rewrite` stays a
    pure REPORTING channel and does NOT add the `d8_pending_rewrite` held_reason. Flag OFF -> the block
    still fires (byte-identical; the 44 existing release_policy/replay tests pass unchanged).
    
    This is the minimal functional fix (one guarded append). The vestigial `rewrite_already_attempted`
    PARAM threading + the intrinsic-self-correction tighter_retry flag-gate (PG_SECTION_REPAIR) are
    follow-up cleanup slices.
    
    Tests (2): flag OFF keeps the block + reports needs_rewrite (byte-identical); flag ON keeps
    needs_rewrite reporting but drops the phantom held_reason.
    
    Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>

+    # hardcoded False at every call site and NO outer loop ever re-runs the seam to set it True
+    # (grep: `rewrite_already_attempted=True` exists ONLY in tests/). So it blocks release for an
+    # attempt the architecture structurally never executes. Under the always-release reframe
+    # (I-perm-001) an UNSUPPORTED claim ships LABELED via the annotator, not blocked, so the phantom
+    # block is removed: when PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE is on, `needs_rewrite` stays a pure REPORTING channel
+    # and does NOT add a held_reason. Flag OFF -> byte-identical (the block still fires).

diff --git a/tests/roles/test_pending_rewrite_iperm006.py b/tests/roles/test_pending_rewrite_iperm006.py

+"""I-perm-006 (#1200) — kill the phantom `d8_pending_rewrite` block under always-release.
+
+`d8_pending_rewrite` fires whenever a non-VERIFIED claim populates `needs_rewrite` AND
+`rewrite_already_attempted` is False — which is ALWAYS (it is hardcoded False at every call site and
+no outer loop ever re-runs the seam to set it True). So it blocks release for a rewrite the
+architecture structurally never executes. Under the always-release reframe (I-perm-001) an
+UNSUPPORTED claim ships LABELED via the annotator, so the phantom block is removed when
+PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE is on; `needs_rewrite` stays a pure REPORTING channel. Flag OFF -> byte-identical.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import pytest
+
+from src.polaris_graph.roles.release_policy import (
+    CoverageLedger,
+    D8ClaimRow,
+    _REASON_PENDING_REWRITE,
+    apply_d8_release_policy,
+)
+
+
+def _decision(monkeypatch, *, always_release: bool):
+    if always_release:
+        monkeypatch.setenv("PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE", "1")
+    else:
+        monkeypatch.delenv("PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE", raising=False)
+    # One material, non-VERIFIED claim -> populates needs_rewrite (rewrite_already_attempted=False,
+    # as every production call site hardcodes).
+    rows = [D8ClaimRow(claim_id="c1", severity="S1", verdict="UNSUPPORTED")]
+    ledger = CoverageLedger(required_element_ids=[], covered_element_ids=set())
+    return apply_d8_release_policy(
+        rows,
+        required_s0_categories=[],
+        coverage_ledger=ledger,
+        coverage_threshold=0.0,
+        rewrite_already_attempted=False,
+    )
+
+
+def test_flag_off_byte_identical_block(monkeypatch):
+    d = _decision(monkeypatch, always_release=False)
+    assert "c1" in d.needs_rewrite, "non-VERIFIED claim must still be reported in needs_rewrite"
+    assert _REASON_PENDING_REWRITE in d.held_reasons, "flag OFF keeps the existing phantom block"
+
+
+def test_always_release_removes_phantom_block(monkeypatch):
+    d = _decision(monkeypatch, always_release=True)
+    # needs_rewrite is UNCHANGED — it stays the pure reporting channel.
+    assert "c1" in d.needs_rewrite
+    # ...but it no longer adds the phantom held_reason, so this claim alone does not block release.
+    assert _REASON_PENDING_REWRITE not in d.held_reasons

1:"""D8 production release policy — occurrence / residual / S0-must-cover gate.
2:
3:I-meta-002 sub-PR-3. This is the PRODUCTION release gate (a pure function over D8 claim
4:rows; no network, no I/O except the config loader). It is a SEPARATE layer from the
5:FROZEN, pre-registered benchmark scorer (`claim_audit_scorer.py`): this module REUSES the
6:canonical `Verdict` vocabulary (for the type hint only) but does NOT mutate the scorer, does
7:NOT import its private constants, and does NOT change its 0.70 frozen benchmark threshold.
8:
9:The clinical occurrence/residual split (from the I-meta-002 iter-2 D8 design ruling):
10:
11:  * FABRICATED is OCCURRENCE-gated with zero tolerance, via a true one-way LATCH. A
12:    fabricated *citation identity* arrives already stamped `verdict=="FABRICATED"` — the
13:    CALLER (sub-PR-5) runs `judge_contract.classify_unreachable` UPSTREAM with the evidence
14:    pool and writes the result into the row. D8 reads `verdict` only; it never re-classifies
15:    and never receives the evidence pool.
16:  * UNSUPPORTED is RESIDUAL-gated: one rewrite/refuse-in-place attempt, then gate only if the
17:    `CoverageLedger` fraction is below the configured `coverage_threshold`. The ledger
18:    denominator is the FIXED per-question required-element set, so dropping/refusing a claim
19:    LOWERS coverage rather than dodging the gate.
20:  * Genuine UNREACHABLE fetch-misses follow the SAME residual path as UNSUPPORTED (never
21:    silently passed). Only fabricated identities (already `FABRICATED`) occurrence-gate.
22:  * S0 must-cover categories abort release if any required category lacks a VERIFIED claim,
23:    regardless of the overall coverage fraction.
24:  * PARTIAL S0/S1 claims get one rewrite attempt, then ship as a visible advisory gap.
25:
26:Refused-in-place / residual gaps are always emitted as visible `Gap`s — never silent drops.

56:_REASON_UNSUPPORTED_RESIDUAL_BELOW_COVERAGE = "d8_unsupported_residual_below_coverage"

58:# (the required attempt has not happened). Blocks release on the first pass (Codex diff P1-a).

83:@dataclass
84:class D8ClaimRow:
85:    """Production-side D8 claim row (wrapper; does NOT mutate the frozen `ClaimRow`).
86:
87:    `verdict` is a `claim_audit_scorer.Verdict` value already stamped by the caller
88:    (sub-PR-5): fabricated citation identity -> "FABRICATED"; genuine fetch-miss ->
89:    "UNREACHABLE". D8 reads it; it never calls `classify_unreachable`.
90:
91:    `citation_id` is carried for gap reporting only. `s0_categories` lists which S0
92:    must-cover categories THIS claim addresses (empty if none).
93:    """
94:
95:    claim_id: str
96:    severity: str
97:    verdict: Verdict
98:    citation_id: str | None = None
99:    s0_categories: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
100:
101:    @property
102:    def is_material(self) -> bool:
103:        return self.severity in _MATERIAL_SEVERITIES
104:
105:
106:@dataclass
107:class CoverageLedger:
108:    """Element-level coverage ledger with a FIXED required-set denominator.
109:
110:    `covered_element_ids` is populated by the CALLER (sub-PR-5) — only required elements
111:    satisfied by a citation-supported VERIFIED claim are added, and genuine UNREACHABLE
112:    elements are excluded by the caller. D8 only reads `.fraction()`. Because the denominator
113:    is the fixed required set, dropping/refusing a claim shrinks the numerator (lowers the
114:    fraction); it can never inflate coverage.
115:    """
116:
117:    required_element_ids: list[str]
118:    covered_element_ids: set[str] = field(default_factory=set)
119:
120:    def fraction(self) -> float:
121:        required = set(self.required_element_ids)
122:        if not required:
123:            return 1.0
124:        return len(required & self.covered_element_ids) / len(required)

127:@dataclass
128:class Gap:
129:    """One visible gap in `gaps.json`. Never a silent drop."""
130:
131:    ref: str  # claim_id or category
132:    kind: str  # one of _GAP_* above
133:    severity: str
134:    note: str

148:@dataclass
149:class D8PolicyConfig:
150:    """Loaded D8 policy config (production layer)."""
151:
152:    coverage_threshold: float
153:    material_severities: list[str]
154:    s0_must_cover_categories: list[str]

156:
157:def load_d8_policy_config(path: str | Path | None = None) -> D8PolicyConfig:
158:    """Load the D8 release-policy config from YAML (LAW VI, zero hard-coding).
159:
160:    Fails loudly (FileNotFoundError / KeyError) on a missing file or missing key — never
161:    silently defaults. The per-question required S0 set is passed by the caller, not read
162:    here; `s0_must_cover_categories` is only the default clinical vocabulary.
163:    """
164:    config_path = Path(path) if path is not None else _DEFAULT_CONFIG_PATH
165:    if not config_path.is_file():
166:        raise FileNotFoundError(f"D8 policy config not found: {config_path}")
167:    with config_path.open(encoding="utf-8") as handle:
168:        data = yaml.safe_load(handle)
169:    if not isinstance(data, dict):
170:        raise ValueError(f"D8 policy config is not a mapping: {config_path}")
171:    return D8PolicyConfig(
172:        coverage_threshold=float(data[_CONFIG_KEY_COVERAGE_THRESHOLD]),
173:        material_severities=list(data[_CONFIG_KEY_MATERIAL_SEVERITIES]),
174:        s0_must_cover_categories=list(data[_CONFIG_KEY_S0_MUST_COVER]),
175:    )
176:
177:
178:def apply_d8_release_policy(
179:    d8_rows: list[D8ClaimRow],
180:    *,
181:    required_s0_categories: list[str],
182:    coverage_ledger: CoverageLedger,
183:    coverage_threshold: float,
184:    rewrite_already_attempted: bool,
185:    prior_fabricated_latched: bool = False,
186:) -> ReleaseDecision:
187:    """Apply the D8 production release policy to one pass of claim rows.
188:
189:    Every gate is evaluated (no short-circuit) so `gaps` / `held_reasons` are complete.
190:    `release_allowed` is True iff `held_reasons` is empty; `gaps` and `needs_rewrite` are
191:    separate reporting channels and do NOT by themselves block release.
192:    """
193:    held_reasons: list[str] = []
194:    gaps: list[Gap] = []
195:    needs_rewrite: list[str] = []
196:
197:    material_rows = [row for row in d8_rows if row.is_material]
198:
199:    # (a) FABRICATED occurrence LATCH — one-way; rewrite does NOT clear it.
200:    fabricated_this_pass = any(
201:        row.verdict == _VERDICT_FABRICATED for row in material_rows
202:    )
203:    fabricated_occurrence_latched = prior_fabricated_latched or fabricated_this_pass
204:    if fabricated_occurrence_latched:
205:        held_reasons.append(_REASON_FABRICATED_OCCURRENCE)
206:
207:    # (b) UNSUPPORTED residual + (b2) genuine UNREACHABLE residual — SAME path.
208:    # First pass: route material UNSUPPORTED/UNREACHABLE rows to a rewrite/refuse-in-place
209:    # attempt. Post-attempt: emit a VISIBLE residual gap for any that remain (never a silent
210:    # drop). The coverage HOLD below is computed from the ledger alone — NOT from whether a
211:    # residual row is still present — so dropping/refusing the row cannot dodge the gate
212:    # (Codex diff P1-b).
213:    for row in material_rows:
214:        if row.verdict not in (_VERDICT_UNSUPPORTED, _VERDICT_UNREACHABLE):
215:            continue
216:        if not rewrite_already_attempted:
217:            needs_rewrite.append(row.claim_id)
218:        else:
219:            if row.verdict == _VERDICT_UNREACHABLE:
220:                note = (
221:                    "genuine fetch-miss (UNREACHABLE) remained after one rewrite attempt; "
222:                    "visible residual gap, not silently passed"
223:                )
224:            else:
225:                note = "unsupported claim remained after one rewrite/refuse-in-place attempt"
226:            gaps.append(
227:                Gap(
228:                    ref=row.claim_id,
229:                    kind=_GAP_RESIDUAL_UNSUPPORTED,
230:                    severity=row.severity,
231:                    note=note,
232:                )
233:            )
234:    # Coverage floor — UNCONDITIONAL on the fixed-denominator ledger. A run whose required-
235:    # element coverage is below threshold is never releasable, whether the shortfall is caused
236:    # by an UNSUPPORTED/UNREACHABLE row that is still present, one that was dropped/refused, or
237:    # a required element that never had a claim at all. This closes the "drop the row to dodge
238:    # the gate" hole (Codex diff P1-b): the denominator is the required set, so removing a claim
239:    # lowers the fraction. On the first pass a low fraction is additionally caught by the
240:    # pending-rewrite hold below; once the rewrite is exhausted, this is the binding gate.
241:    if coverage_ledger.fraction() < coverage_threshold:
242:        held_reasons.append(_REASON_UNSUPPORTED_RESIDUAL_BELOW_COVERAGE)
243:        gaps.append(
244:            Gap(
245:                ref="__coverage__",
246:                kind=_GAP_COVERAGE_SHORTFALL,
247:                severity="S0",
248:                note=(
249:                    f"required-element coverage {coverage_ledger.fraction():.3f} is below the "
250:                    f"{coverage_threshold:.3f} threshold (fixed required-set denominator)"
251:                ),
252:            )
253:        )
254:
255:    # (c) S0 must-cover gate — category covered iff a VERIFIED claim carries it.
256:    verified_categories: set[str] = set()
257:    for row in d8_rows:
258:        if row.verdict == _VERDICT_VERIFIED:
259:            verified_categories.update(row.s0_categories)
260:    for category in required_s0_categories:
261:        if category not in verified_categories:
262:            held_reasons.append(f"{_REASON_S0_MUST_COVER_MISSING_PREFIX}{category}")
263:            gaps.append(
264:                Gap(
265:                    ref=category,
266:                    kind=_GAP_UNCOVERED_S0,
267:                    severity="S0",
268:                    note=(
269:                        "required S0 must-cover category has no VERIFIED claim "
270:                        "(PARTIAL/citation-only does not satisfy it)"
271:                    ),
272:                )
273:            )
274:
275:    # (d) PARTIAL S0/S1 — one rewrite, then visible advisory gap.
276:    for row in d8_rows:
277:        if row.verdict != _VERDICT_PARTIAL:
278:            continue
279:        if row.severity not in _PARTIAL_REWRITE_SEVERITIES:
280:            continue
281:        if not rewrite_already_attempted:
282:            needs_rewrite.append(row.claim_id)
283:        else:
284:            gaps.append(
285:                Gap(
286:                    ref=row.claim_id,
287:                    kind=_GAP_PARTIAL_ADVISORY,
288:                    severity=row.severity,
289:                    note="PARTIAL claim ships as a visible advisory after one rewrite attempt",
290:                )
291:            )
292:
293:    # A pass with pending rewrites is NOT releasable — the required rewrite/refuse-in-place
294:    # attempt has not happened yet (Codex diff P1-a: release_allowed previously ignored
295:    # needs_rewrite, letting a first-pass run release before the attempt).
296:    #
297:    # I-perm-006 (#1200): `d8_pending_rewrite` is a PHANTOM block — `rewrite_already_attempted` is
298:    # hardcoded False at every call site and NO outer loop ever re-runs the seam to set it True
299:    # (grep: `rewrite_already_attempted=True` exists ONLY in tests/). So it blocks release for an
300:    # attempt the architecture structurally never executes. Under the always-release reframe
301:    # (I-perm-001) an UNSUPPORTED claim ships LABELED via the annotator, not blocked, so the phantom
302:    # block is removed: when PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE is on, `needs_rewrite` stays a pure REPORTING channel
303:    # and does NOT add a held_reason. Flag OFF -> byte-identical (the block still fires).
304:    if needs_rewrite and not always_release_enabled():
305:        held_reasons.append(_REASON_PENDING_REWRITE)
306:
307:    release_allowed = not held_reasons
308:    return ReleaseDecision(
309:        release_allowed=release_allowed,
310:        held_reasons=held_reasons,
311:        gaps=gaps,
312:        needs_rewrite=needs_rewrite,
313:        fabricated_occurrence_latched=fabricated_occurrence_latched,
314:    )
315:
316:
317:def to_gaps_json(decision: ReleaseDecision) -> list[dict]:
318:    """Serialize a decision's gaps into a JSON-ready list of dicts (gaps.json structure)."""
319:    return [
320:        {
321:            "ref": gap.ref,
322:            "kind": gap.kind,
323:            "severity": gap.severity,
324:            "note": gap.note,
325:        }
326:        for gap in decision.gaps
327:    ]

329:
330:# ── I-perm-001 (#1195) keystone slice 1: WITHHOLD → ALWAYS-RELEASE + LABEL ───────────────────
331:# The withhold-when-imperfect gate stack (coverage-below-threshold, S0-must-cover-missing,
332:# pending-rewrite) BLOCKS the whole report. Under always-release it converts every such hold
333:# from a release-BLOCKER into a DISPLAYED disclosed-gap label; the report ships with honest
334:# per-gap disclosure and the user judges. The ONLY hard line that still withholds a normal
335:# report is (a) a FABRICATED occurrence latch, or (b) true zero-grounding (no VERIFIED claim AND
336:# no usable evidence). A clinical safety floor (all required S0 SAFETY categories disclosed as
337:# gaps / zero VERIFIED safety content) does not HARD-block, but it blocks the NORMAL render and
338:# ships an honest "insufficient safety evidence" report instead (operator decision, blueprint R2).
339:#
340:# DEFAULT OFF: PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE unset/0/false/no/off -> compute_release_outcome reproduces the
341:# legacy `release_allowed` decision verbatim (byte-identical; no status/label change).
342:
343:# Master flag (default OFF -> legacy withhold behaviour, byte-identical). ON only on an EXPLICIT
344:# truthy token (Codex slice-1 P2: a stray value like "garbage" must NOT silently enable it).
345:_ENV_ALWAYS_RELEASE = "PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE"
346:_ON_VALUES = frozenset({"1", "true", "yes", "on"})
347:
348:# Held reasons that are NON-hard: under always-release they become disclosed-gap labels, not
349:# release blockers. A FABRICATED occurrence is the one held reason that is NEVER a mere label.
350:_NON_HARD_HELD_REASONS = frozenset(
351:    {
352:        _REASON_UNSUPPORTED_RESIDUAL_BELOW_COVERAGE,
353:        _REASON_PENDING_REWRITE,
354:    }
355:)
356:
357:# Status vocabulary (mirrors scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES; slice 1 adds
358:# the two released-with-disclosure terminals — both are RELEASED, not abort).
359:STATUS_SUCCESS = "success"
360:STATUS_RELEASED_WITH_DISCLOSED_GAPS = "released_with_disclosed_gaps"
361:STATUS_RELEASED_INSUFFICIENT_SAFETY = "released_insufficient_safety_evidence"
362:STATUS_ABORT_NO_VERIFIED = "abort_no_verified_sections"
363:STATUS_ABORT_FOUR_ROLE_HELD = "abort_four_role_release_held"
364:STATUS_ABORT_FABRICATED = "abort_evaluator_critical"
365:
366:
367:def is_hard_block(
368:    *,
369:    fabricated_occurrence_latched: bool,
370:    zero_verified: bool,
371:    zero_usable_evidence: bool,
372:) -> bool:
373:    """The canonical no-fabrication hard line (blueprint R1): a report is HARD-blocked iff a
374:    FABRICATED occurrence latched OR there is true zero-grounding (no VERIFIED claim AND no usable
375:    evidence). Everything else releases (with labels) under always-release."""
376:    return bool(fabricated_occurrence_latched or (zero_verified and zero_usable_evidence))
377:
378:
379:@dataclass
380:class ReleaseOutcome:
381:    """The always-release-aware release outcome over a D8 ``ReleaseDecision`` (I-perm-001).
382:
383:    ``released`` — a report ships (normal OR honest-insufficient-safety variant).
384:    ``hard_block`` — the no-fabrication hard line fired; NO report ships as clean.
385:    ``normal_release_blocked`` — the polished normal report is withheld (hard_block OR the clinical
386:        safety floor is insufficient), but an honest report may still ship.
387:    ``status`` — the terminal pipeline status.
388:    ``disclosed_gaps`` — the held reasons surfaced as DISPLAYED labels (not blockers).
389:    ``release_quality_score`` — the displayed coverage fraction (NOT a trap-door threshold).
390:    """
391:
392:    released: bool
393:    hard_block: bool
394:    normal_release_blocked: bool
395:    status: str
396:    disclosed_gaps: list[str]
397:    hard_block_reasons: list[str]
398:    release_quality_score: float
399:    safety_floor: str  # "ok" | "insufficient"
400:
401:
402:def always_release_enabled() -> bool:
403:    """PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE (default OFF). ON only on explicit truthy ('1'/'true'/'yes'/'on')."""
404:    import os
405:
406:    return os.environ.get(_ENV_ALWAYS_RELEASE, "").strip().lower() in _ON_VALUES
407:
408:
409:def compute_release_outcome(
410:    decision: ReleaseDecision,
411:    *,
412:    zero_verified: bool,
413:    zero_usable_evidence: bool,
414:    safety_floor_insufficient: bool,
415:    coverage_fraction: float,
416:    always_release: bool | None = None,
417:) -> ReleaseOutcome:
418:    """Map a D8 ``ReleaseDecision`` to a release outcome under the always-release reframe.
419:
420:    When always-release is OFF (default), reproduce the LEGACY decision verbatim: ``released`` ==
421:    ``decision.release_allowed``, the held reasons stay blockers, and the status is the legacy
422:    held/success label — byte-identical behaviour. When ON, convert non-hard holds to disclosed
423:    gaps and release, keeping only the fabricated/zero-grounding hard line and the clinical
424:    safety-floor normal-render block (blueprint R1/R2).
425:    """
426:    enabled = always_release_enabled() if always_release is None else always_release
427:    hard_block = is_hard_block(
428:        fabricated_occurrence_latched=decision.fabricated_occurrence_latched,
429:        zero_verified=zero_verified,
430:        zero_usable_evidence=zero_usable_evidence,
431:    )
432:    hard_block_reasons: list[str] = []
433:    if decision.fabricated_occurrence_latched:
434:        hard_block_reasons.append(_REASON_FABRICATED_OCCURRENCE)
435:    if zero_verified and zero_usable_evidence:
436:        hard_block_reasons.append("zero_grounding")
437:    safety_floor = "insufficient" if safety_floor_insufficient else "ok"
438:
439:    if not enabled:
440:        # Legacy withhold path — byte-identical to `decision.release_allowed`.
441:        status = STATUS_SUCCESS if decision.release_allowed else STATUS_ABORT_FOUR_ROLE_HELD
442:        return ReleaseOutcome(
443:            released=decision.release_allowed,
444:            hard_block=not decision.release_allowed and hard_block,
445:            normal_release_blocked=not decision.release_allowed,
446:            status=status,
447:            disclosed_gaps=[],
448:            hard_block_reasons=hard_block_reasons if not decision.release_allowed else [],
449:            release_quality_score=coverage_fraction,
450:            safety_floor=safety_floor,
451:        )
452:
453:    # --- always-release ON ---
454:    if hard_block:
455:        status = (
456:            STATUS_ABORT_FABRICATED
457:            if decision.fabricated_occurrence_latched
458:            else STATUS_ABORT_NO_VERIFIED
459:        )
460:        return ReleaseOutcome(
461:            released=False,
462:            hard_block=True,
463:            normal_release_blocked=True,
464:            status=status,
465:            # A hard-block reason (fabricated) is NEVER a disclosed GAP (Codex slice-1 P2): it
466:            # lives in hard_block_reasons. Surface only the non-hard holds as disclosed gaps.
467:            disclosed_gaps=[
468:                r for r in decision.held_reasons if r != _REASON_FABRICATED_OCCURRENCE
469:            ],
470:            hard_block_reasons=hard_block_reasons,
471:            release_quality_score=coverage_fraction,
472:            safety_floor=safety_floor,
473:        )
474:
475:    # Every remaining held reason is a DISPLAYED disclosed-gap label, not a blocker.
476:    disclosed_gaps = list(decision.held_reasons)
477:    if safety_floor_insufficient:
478:        # Clinical safety floor: ship the honest insufficient-safety report, block normal render.
479:        return ReleaseOutcome(
480:            released=True,
481:            hard_block=False,
482:            normal_release_blocked=True,
483:            status=STATUS_RELEASED_INSUFFICIENT_SAFETY,
484:            disclosed_gaps=disclosed_gaps,
485:            hard_block_reasons=[],
486:            release_quality_score=coverage_fraction,
487:            safety_floor="insufficient",
488:        )
489:    status = STATUS_SUCCESS if not disclosed_gaps else STATUS_RELEASED_WITH_DISCLOSED_GAPS
490:    return ReleaseOutcome(
491:        released=True,
492:        hard_block=False,
493:        normal_release_blocked=False,
494:        status=status,
495:        disclosed_gaps=disclosed_gaps,
496:        hard_block_reasons=[],
497:        release_quality_score=coverage_fraction,
498:        safety_floor="ok",
499:    )

9:flat result the sweep maps onto the manifest + `VerifiedSentence.evaluator_agrees`.

143:    gate). `coverage_fraction` is the canonical-denominator coverage actually achieved.

161:def evaluator_agrees_from_verdict(final_verdict: str) -> bool:
162:    """Map a composed final verdict to the two-family `evaluator_agrees` boolean.
163:
164:    VERIFIED -> True (the evaluator stack confirms the claim); every other verdict
165:    (PARTIAL / UNSUPPORTED / FABRICATED / UNREACHABLE) -> False. The sweep applies this ONLY
166:    to kept sentences (`verifier_pass=True`), so the `VerifiedSentence` validator that forbids
167:    `evaluator_agrees=True` on a dropped sentence is never tripped.
168:    """
169:    return final_verdict == _VERDICT_VERIFIED
170:
171:
172:def build_evaluator_agrees_map(
173:    final_verdicts: dict[str, str],
174:    kept_claim_ids: set[str] | None = None,
175:) -> dict[str, bool]:
176:    """Build the per-claim `evaluator_agrees` MAP for the sweep manifest (I-meta-002 PR-9/M5).
177:
178:    Maps each `claim_id` in `final_verdicts` to the §-1.1 fail-safe boolean:
179:
180:        evaluator_agrees = (claim is kept) AND evaluator_agrees_from_verdict(final_verdict)
181:
182:    where `evaluator_agrees_from_verdict` is the SINGLE source of the verdict rule
183:    (`final_verdict == "VERIFIED"`). Every other verdict — PARTIAL / UNSUPPORTED / FABRICATED /
184:    UNREACHABLE / any unknown string — maps to False. The value is NEVER True before a VERIFIED
185:    final verdict exists AND the claim is kept (a non-VERIFIED verdict must never read as
186:    "evaluator agreed" in clinical context).
187:
188:    `kept_claim_ids` is the set of claim_ids that survived as kept/verified sentences
189:    (`verifier_pass=True`). When it is None, ALL claim_ids in `final_verdicts` are treated as
190:    kept — INVARIANT: on the sweep path the `FourRoleClaim` set is built (by the M3a builder)
191:    from KEPT (is_verified) sentences only, so every claim_id in `final_verdicts` is already a
192:    kept claim and passing None is correct there. When a set IS supplied, a claim_id absent from
193:    it maps to False even if its verdict is VERIFIED (defensive: a not-kept claim can never agree).
194:
195:    Keys are EXACTLY `final_verdicts.keys()` (so the map is joinable to
196:    `four_role_claim_audit.json` from M3b); `kept_claim_ids` affects only the boolean value and
197:    never adds or removes keys. An empty `final_verdicts` yields `{}` (no error here; the sweep
198:    branch's own fail-closed guards already handle empty claim sets upstream).
199:    """
200:    agrees_map: dict[str, bool] = {}
201:    for claim_id, final_verdict in final_verdicts.items():
202:        is_kept = kept_claim_ids is None or claim_id in kept_claim_ids
203:        agrees_map[claim_id] = is_kept and evaluator_agrees_from_verdict(final_verdict)
204:    return agrees_map

207:def _write_role_call_log(path: Path, role_call_log: list[dict]) -> None:
208:    """Write the per-role-call reasoning log as one sorted-key JSON object per line.
209:
210:    I-run11-001 (#1042): factored out of `run_four_role_evaluation` so the SAME serialization is
211:    used by both the INCREMENTAL per-claim write (mid-run monitorability) and the final idempotent
212:    write. Byte-identical to the prior inline `write_text` (`ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True`),
213:    so a partial file rewritten on the next claim is just a longer prefix of the same content.
214:    """
215:    path.write_text(
216:        "".join(
217:            json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True) + "\n"
218:            for entry in role_call_log
219:        ),
220:        encoding="utf-8",
221:    )

223:
224:def _compute_claim_results(
225:    transport: RoleTransport,
226:    *,
227:    claims: list[FourRoleClaim],
228:    model_slugs: dict[str, str],
229:    timestamp: str,
230:    run_dir: Path,
231:    heartbeat_claims_cb=None,
232:) -> list[tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float | None]]:
233:    """COMPUTE the per-claim 4-role pipeline for every claim, returning results BY INPUT INDEX.
234:
235:    I-run11-001 (#1042), Codex Path-B SAFE design (.codex/I-run11-seam). This is the ONLY half
236:    that runs the (already-paid) verifier calls; it makes NO reduction decision — the parent
237:    reduces in input order. Each element is `(ClaimPipelineResult, cost_delta)` for `claims[idx]`,
238:    where:
239:
240:      * SEQUENTIAL (`_CLAIM_WORKERS == 1` or a single claim): `run_claim_pipeline` is called
241:        DIRECTLY on the parent thread (no copied context, no `reset_run_cost`), so
242:        `RecordingTransport.complete()` enforces the LIVE per-call run budget on the parent
243:        `_RUN_COST_CTX` EXACTLY as today. `cost_delta is None` signals the parent "already
244:        accounted — do not re-add" (byte-equivalence with the pre-#1042 behaviour).
245:
246:      * PARALLEL: each claim runs inside its OWN `contextvars.copy_context()` snapshot that is taken
247:        ON THE PARENT THREAD BEFORE submit (Codex iter-2 P1.2 — copying inside the worker would
248:        snapshot the worker's EMPTY default context, so the parent Path-B capture sink
249:        `pathB_capture._SINK` / `_ROLE` registered by `pathB_runner` on the PARENT would be ABSENT
250:        and verifier capture would no-op, failing post-run completeness when workers>1). Each claim
251:        gets its OWN copy (never one shared copy across concurrent workers — a copy carries the
252:        worker's isolated `_RUN_COST_CTX` AND the parent's `_SINK` reference). The worker
253:        `reset_run_cost()`s its copy, runs the pipeline, and returns `current_run_cost()` as
254:        `cost_delta`; the PARENT re-adds it to the single run counter and enforces the cap DURING
255:        compute (Codex iter-2 P1.1) so overspend is bounded to the workers in-flight at breach
256:        (~workers-1), not all claims. The pathB capture `_SINK` is shared BY REFERENCE through the
257:        copied context (atomic `list.append`), so verifier captures land at the PARENT sink for the
258:        M4 gate — it is NOT isolated. A worker exception PROPAGATES (fail closed; no `except: pass`).
259:    """
260:    n = len(claims)
261:
262:    # I-ready-017 FX-08b (#1113): CLAIM-LEVEL DEDUP (BUG-04 determinism half).
263:    # 4+ byte-identical claims were SPLIT VERIFIED/UNSUPPORTED in the same run
264:    # (a non-deterministic release gate). Two claims whose ENTIRE pipeline INPUT
265:    # is identical MUST get the same verdict — so run the pipeline ONCE per
266:    # distinct input and fan the verdict out. The key is the FULL input the
267:    # pipeline consumes (claim_text + evidence doc_id+text + severity +
268:    # s0_categories), NOT just (sentence+ids+spans): anything that could
269:    # legitimately change the verdict is in the key, so two genuinely-different
270:    # claims can NEVER collapse to one verdict (faithfulness-safe; identical
271:    # input => identical output is the only justification for sharing a verdict).
272:    # The evidence doc `text` is the FX-03 cited WINDOW, so it encodes the span.
273:    # Fan-out is HONEST on the audit trail + cost: a duplicate gets its OWN
274:    # claim_id (dataclasses.replace on d8_row), the SHARED verdict + sub-results,
275:    # EMPTY records (no new model calls were made for it, so all_records /
276:    # role_call_log are not inflated), and zero cost (cost_delta None). Coverage
277:    # credit still flows per-claim (each dup's covered_element_ids on its VERIFIED
278:    # verdict). Flag-gated (PG_FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_DEDUP, default ON); OFF reverts to
279:    # the per-claim run. Recursion on representatives is one level deep (reps have
280:    # all-distinct keys -> this branch is skipped on the inner call).
281:    _dedup_enabled = os.getenv("PG_FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_DEDUP", "1") != "0"
282:
283:    def _dedup_key(c: FourRoleClaim) -> tuple:
284:        return (
285:            " ".join((c.claim_text or "").split()),
286:            tuple(sorted(
287:                (d.doc_id, d.text) for d in (c.evidence_documents or [])
288:            )),
289:            c.severity,
290:            tuple(sorted(c.s0_categories or [])),
291:        )
292:
293:    if _dedup_enabled and n > 1:
294:        rep_idx_by_key: dict[tuple, int] = {}
295:        rep_indices: list[int] = []
296:        for idx, claim in enumerate(claims):
297:            k = _dedup_key(claim)
298:            if k not in rep_idx_by_key:
299:                rep_idx_by_key[k] = idx
300:                rep_indices.append(idx)
301:        if len(rep_indices) < n:
302:            # At least one duplicate — run the pipeline only on representatives.
303:            rep_results = _compute_claim_results(
304:                transport,
305:                claims=[claims[i] for i in rep_indices],
306:                model_slugs=model_slugs,
307:                timestamp=timestamp,
308:                run_dir=run_dir,
309:                heartbeat_claims_cb=heartbeat_claims_cb,  # Codex AC1-gate P2-1: dedup path too
310:            )
311:            rep_result_by_idx = {
312:                rep_indices[j]: rep_results[j] for j in range(len(rep_indices))
313:            }
314:            fanned: list[tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float | None]] = []
315:            for idx, claim in enumerate(claims):
316:                rep_idx = rep_idx_by_key[_dedup_key(claim)]
317:                rep_res, rep_cost = rep_result_by_idx[rep_idx]
318:                if idx == rep_idx:
319:                    fanned.append((rep_res, rep_cost))
320:                else:
321:                    # Fan the verdict out to this duplicate under ITS own
322:                    # claim_id; no new model calls (records=[]) and no new spend
323:                    # (cost None) — the representative already paid + recorded.
324:                    dup_row = replace(rep_res.d8_row, claim_id=claim.claim_id)
325:                    dup_res = replace(rep_res, d8_row=dup_row, records=[])
326:                    fanned.append((dup_res, None))
327:            return fanned
328:
329:    def _compute_one(
330:        idx: int, claim: FourRoleClaim, worker_ctx: contextvars.Context
331:    ) -> tuple[int, ClaimPipelineResult, float]:
332:        def _run() -> tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float]:
333:            # Isolate THIS claim's verifier spend in the copied context so the parent can re-add a
334:            # clean per-claim delta and enforce the cap deterministically at the claim boundary.
335:            # `reset_run_cost()` zeroes ONLY this copy's `_RUN_COST_CTX`; the parent's `_SINK` /
336:            # `_ROLE` references carried by the same copy are untouched, so verifier capture lands
337:            # at the parent sink.
338:            reset_run_cost()
339:            res = run_claim_pipeline(
340:                transport,
341:                claim_id=claim.claim_id,
342:                claim=claim.claim_text,
343:                evidence_documents=claim.evidence_documents,
344:                severity=claim.severity,
345:                s0_categories=claim.s0_categories,
346:                model_slugs=model_slugs,
347:                timestamp=timestamp,
348:            )
349:            return res, current_run_cost()
350:
351:        # Run inside the PARENT-captured context snapshot (P1.2): the worker executes `_run` under
352:        # the parent's Path-B capture state, not the worker thread's empty default context.
353:        result, delta = worker_ctx.run(_run)
354:        return idx, result, delta
355:
356:    # SEQUENTIAL fast path: byte-equivalent to the pre-#1042 loop (live per-call budget preserved,
357:    # cost_delta None so the parent does not re-account). A single claim also takes this path (a
358:    # thread pool for one item is pure overhead).
359:    if _CLAIM_WORKERS == 1 or n <= 1:
360:        out: list[tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float | None]] = []
361:        for claim in claims:
362:            result = run_claim_pipeline(
363:                transport,
364:                claim_id=claim.claim_id,
365:                claim=claim.claim_text,
366:                evidence_documents=claim.evidence_documents,
367:                severity=claim.severity,
368:                s0_categories=claim.s0_categories,
369:                model_slugs=model_slugs,
370:                timestamp=timestamp,
371:            )
372:            out.append((result, None))
373:        return out
374:
375:    # PARALLEL path (Codex iter-2 P1.1 + P1.2): enforce the run budget DURING compute, not after the
376:    # whole pool drains. Each claim is submitted with its OWN parent-captured context snapshot so the
377:    # worker inherits the Path-B capture sink/role registered on the parent. We iterate
378:    # `as_completed` and, for each completed future, re-add the worker's per-claim verifier delta to
379:    # the SINGLE parent run counter and re-check the cap — so a cumulative cap breach raises after
380:    # only ~(workers-in-flight) claims have spent, NOT all n. The pool is managed MANUALLY (not via
381:    # `with`, whose `__exit__` waits for ALL pending futures) so on a breach / worker exception we
382:    # `shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)` to cancel still-queued claims, then re-raise
383:    # (P2.2 cancel-on-fail).
384:    #
385:    # P2.1 (aborted-run cost under-accounting — documented, not over-engineered): on a worker
386:    # exception the worker's partial paid spend lives in the worker's isolated copied context and is
387:    # NOT reconciled into the parent counter. This is the SAME accepted tradeoff the seam-timeout
388:    # wrapper documents (run_honest_sweep_r3.py ~L4587-4596: in-flight verifier cost on the
389:    # held/aborted path is not reconciled) — prompt fail-closed termination outranks exact accounting
390:    # on an already-aborted run, and the operator authorized the spend.
391:    computed: list[tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float | None] | None] = [None] * n
392:    # Codex iter-2 P1 (REGRESSION FIX): the progress write below targets `run_dir`, but
393:    # `_compute_claim_results` runs BEFORE `VerifiedClaimGraphStore(run_dir=...)` (which is what
394:    # historically created `run_dir`). Existing callers (scripts/dr_benchmark/offline_e2e.py,
395:    # tests/dr_benchmark/test_offline_e2e.py) pass a `run_dir` that does NOT yet exist, so the
396:    # parallel path's progress write raised FileNotFoundError. Ensure the dir exists exactly once
397:    # at the TOP of the parallel branch (idempotent; the later kg_store reuses the same dir —
398:    # harmless). The SEQUENTIAL fast path does NOT mkdir (it writes no progress file) so it stays
399:    # byte-equivalent to the pre-#1042 behaviour.
400:    run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
401:    progress_path = run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_COMPUTE_PROGRESS_FILENAME
402:    done = 0
403:    pool = concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=_CLAIM_WORKERS)
404:    try:
405:        futures = [
406:            pool.submit(_compute_one, idx, claim, contextvars.copy_context())
407:            for idx, claim in enumerate(claims)
408:        ]
409:        for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(futures):
410:            # `future.result()` re-raises any worker exception (fail closed) — handled below.
411:            idx, result, delta = future.result()
412:            computed[idx] = (result, delta)
413:            # P2.3 + Codex iter-2 P2 (observability): write the tiny on-disk progress marker BEFORE
414:            # the budget enforcement below, so the just-completed claim — INCLUDING a cap-breaching
415:            # one — is reflected in four_role_compute_progress.json even when the very next
416:            # check_run_budget(0) raises BudgetExceededError. `done` counts completed claims
417:            # including the current one. Parent-only write — never inside a worker. A hung compute
418:            # is thus visible on disk DURING compute (the role_call_log only grows during the later,
419:            # parent-only reduction).
420:            done += 1
421:            progress_path.write_text(
422:                json.dumps({"done": done, "total": n}, sort_keys=True) + "\n",
423:                encoding="utf-8",
424:            )
425:            # Enforce the run budget DURING compute (P1.1): thread this claim's verifier spend into
426:            # the SINGLE parent run counter and re-check the cap immediately. A `BudgetExceededError`
427:            # here bounds overspend to the workers in-flight at the breach (~workers-1), not all n.
428:            if delta is not None:
429:                _add_run_cost(delta)
430:                check_run_budget(0)  # raises BudgetExceededError if the cap is now exceeded.
431:            # I-obs-001 #1141 AC1 (Codex AC1-gate P2): forward done/total to the run-status heartbeat
432:            # AFTER _add_run_cost so running_cost_usd reflects the just-completed claim. The progress
433:            # marker above already recorded this claim BEFORE the budget check (cap-breach visibility);
434:            # if check_run_budget raised, the terminal heartbeat captures the abort. Opaque callback —
435:            # sweep_integration stays ignorant of the heartbeat schema; additive, never raises.
436:            if heartbeat_claims_cb is not None:
437:                try:
438:                    heartbeat_claims_cb(done, n)
439:                except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
440:                    pass
441:    except BaseException:
442:        # On ANY failure (BudgetExceededError from the cap OR a propagated worker exception) cancel
443:        # still-pending claims and tear the pool down NON-BLOCKING (P2.2), then re-raise so the
444:        # existing budget-abort / fail-closed path in run_four_role_evaluation handles it. No
445:        # `except: pass` — the error always propagates.
446:        pool.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)
447:        raise
448:    else:
449:        pool.shutdown(wait=True)
450:
451:    # Defensive: every index must be filled (a None here would mean a future silently dropped — a
452:    # real bug, never a vacuous pass). Fail loud rather than reduce a partial result set.
453:    for idx, item in enumerate(computed):
454:        if item is None:
455:            raise RuntimeError(
456:                f"run_four_role_evaluation: claim index {idx} produced no result from the "
457:                f"compute pool (fail-closed — a dropped future must never reduce silently)."
458:            )
459:    return [item for item in computed if item is not None]
460:
461:
462:def run_four_role_evaluation(
463:    transport: RoleTransport,
464:    *,
465:    claims: list[FourRoleClaim],
466:    run_dir: Path,
467:    timestamp: str,
468:    coverage_ledger: CoverageLedger,
469:    required_s0_categories: list[str],
470:    model_slugs: dict[str, str],
471:    rewrite_already_attempted: bool = False,
472:    d8_config_path: str | Path | None = None,
473:    campaign_kg_db: str | Path | None = None,
474:    heartbeat_claims_cb=None,
475:) -> FourRoleEvaluationResult:
476:    """Drive the per-claim 4-role pipeline, apply the SINGLE binding D8 gate, persist the KG.
477:
478:    I-meta-002-q1d (#948): when `campaign_kg_db` is given, the snowball KG is persisted to that
479:    CAMPAIGN-scoped sqlite path (shared across the sweep's questions) instead of the per-question
480:    `run_dir`, so question N can reuse questions 1..N-1's VERIFIED claims. Default None preserves the
481:    per-`run_dir` behavior (existing callers/tests unchanged). The sweep runs questions sequentially, so
482:    there are no concurrent writers; anti-poisoning (only VERIFIED rows reusable) is unchanged.
483:
484:    Pure orchestration over the INJECTED `transport` (no network, no spend). For EACH claim:
485:    run `run_claim_pipeline`, collect its `D8ClaimRow` + served-identity records + final
486:    verdict, and — only on a VERIFIED final verdict — credit that claim's canonical
487:    `covered_element_ids` into the ledger. Then run `apply_d8_release_policy` ONCE over the
488:    collected rows (D8 is the headline gate) and write every per-claim outcome to the snowball
489:    `VerifiedClaimGraphStore` under `run_dir`.
490:
491:    Fail-closed guards (Codex P2): raises `ValueError` on an empty claim set, an empty
492:    canonical required-element denominator, a blank/duplicate `claim_id`, or a missing role
493:    slug — never a vacuous pass and never a synthesized id.
494:    """
495:    # (P2) NO vacuous pass: an empty claim set or an empty canonical coverage denominator must
496:    # fail LOUD here, before any D8 call — fraction()==1.0 over an empty required set would
497:    # otherwise release "nothing" as all-clear.
498:    if not claims:
499:        raise ValueError(
500:            "run_four_role_evaluation: no claims supplied; a 4-role evaluation over zero "
501:            "claims cannot produce a release decision (fail-closed, no vacuous pass)."
502:        )
503:    if not coverage_ledger.required_element_ids:
504:        raise ValueError(
505:            "run_four_role_evaluation: coverage_ledger.required_element_ids is empty; the "
506:            "coverage denominator MUST be the canonical per-question required-element set "
507:            "(fail-closed, no vacuous pass over an empty denominator)."
508:        )
509:    # (Codex sub-PR-6 diff P1, LETHAL safety invariant) The coverage NUMERATOR must be rebuilt
510:    # here SOLELY from VERIFIED final verdicts — never trusted from the caller. A prefilled
511:    # `covered_element_ids` would let a Sentinel-UNGROUNDED claim that we correctly downgrade to
512:    # UNSUPPORTED still ride pre-credited coverage and release. Reject a non-empty incoming set
513:    # (fail LOUD), then credit a FRESH internal ledger only on VERIFIED finals below.
514:    if coverage_ledger.covered_element_ids:
515:        raise ValueError(
516:            "run_four_role_evaluation: coverage_ledger.covered_element_ids must be EMPTY on "
517:            "input; the coverage numerator is rebuilt here from VERIFIED final verdicts only, so "
518:            "a prefilled numerator cannot let an ungrounded/downgraded claim ride pre-credited "
519:            "coverage (fail-closed)."
520:        )
521:    internal_ledger = CoverageLedger(
522:        required_element_ids=list(coverage_ledger.required_element_ids),
523:        covered_element_ids=set(),
524:    )
525:    missing_slugs = [key for key in _REQUIRED_ROLE_SLUG_KEYS if not model_slugs.get(key)]
526:    if missing_slugs:
527:        raise ValueError(
528:            f"run_four_role_evaluation: model_slugs missing required role slug(s) "
529:            f"{missing_slugs}; the pipeline needs mirror/sentinel/judge pins."
530:        )
531:
532:    # (P2) NO synthesized ids: every claim must carry a non-blank, unique existing claim_id.
533:    seen_ids: set[str] = set()
534:    for claim in claims:
535:        claim_id = (claim.claim_id or "").strip()
536:        if not claim_id:
537:            raise ValueError(
538:                "run_four_role_evaluation: a claim has a blank claim_id; claim_ids are "
539:                "caller-supplied (verified-sentence / section ids) and never synthesized."
540:            )
541:        if claim_id in seen_ids:
542:            raise ValueError(
543:                f"run_four_role_evaluation: duplicate claim_id {claim_id!r}; ids must be "
544:                f"unique so rewrite/gap traceability does not collide."
545:            )
546:        seen_ids.add(claim_id)
547:
548:    d8_rows: list[D8ClaimRow] = []
549:    all_records: list[RoleCallRecord] = []
550:    final_verdicts: dict[str, str] = {}
551:    # I-meta-002-q1b (#939): per-role-call reasoning log, persisted to four_role_role_calls.jsonl
552:    # for line-by-line review. `reasoning` is its OWN field — NEVER concatenated into the verdict.
553:    role_call_log: list[dict] = []
554:
555:    # I-run11-001 (#1042): COMPUTE the per-claim pipeline (possibly in parallel), then REDUCE on
556:    # the parent thread in ORIGINAL claim order. `computed[idx]` holds `(ClaimPipelineResult,
557:    # cost_delta)` for `claims[idx]`; `cost_delta` is the per-claim verifier spend captured INSIDE
558:    # the worker's isolated `_RUN_COST_CTX` (parallel path) or None (sequential path, where
559:    # RecordingTransport already enforced the LIVE per-call budget on the parent counter).
560:    # Codex iter-2 P1.1: the PARALLEL path now ENFORCES the run-budget cap DURING compute (each
561:    # claim's delta is re-added to the parent counter and the cap re-checked as its future
562:    # completes), so a cap breach raises after only ~(workers-in-flight) claims have spent — the
563:    # reduction below NO LONGER re-adds `cost_delta` (it would double-count). `cost_delta` is kept
564:    # in the returned tuples for audit only.
565:    computed: list[tuple[ClaimPipelineResult, float | None]] = _compute_claim_results(
566:        transport,
567:        claims=claims,
568:        model_slugs=model_slugs,
569:        timestamp=timestamp,
570:        run_dir=run_dir,
571:        heartbeat_claims_cb=heartbeat_claims_cb,
572:    )
573:
574:    role_calls_path = run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_ROLE_CALLS_FILENAME
575:
576:    # I-meta-002-q1d (#948): campaign-scoped KG when given, else per-question run_dir (default).
577:    kg_store = (
578:        VerifiedClaimGraphStore(db_path=campaign_kg_db)
579:        if campaign_kg_db is not None
580:        else VerifiedClaimGraphStore(run_dir=run_dir)
581:    )
582:    try:
583:        # Reduce in INPUT order (zip over claims + the index-ordered `computed` list). Completion
584:        # order NEVER drives any reduction — the parallel path collected results BY INDEX, so this
585:        # is byte-identical to the sequential reduction regardless of which claim finished first.
586:        # Codex iter-2 P1.1: the run-budget cap is now enforced DURING compute inside
587:        # `_compute_claim_results` (parallel path) — the per-claim `cost_delta` was ALREADY re-added
588:        # to the parent counter and the cap re-checked there. This reduction is therefore PARENT-only
589:        # and budget-NEUTRAL: it touches ONLY d8_rows / all_records / final_verdicts / role_call_log /
590:        # coverage / kg_store.write_claim / the incremental log. `cost_delta` is retained in the tuple
591:        # for audit but is NOT re-added here (re-adding would double-count the verifier spend).
592:        for claim, (result, _cost_delta) in zip(claims, computed):
593:            d8_rows.append(result.d8_row)
594:            all_records.extend(result.records)
595:            final_verdicts[claim.claim_id] = result.final_verdict
596:            # I-meta-002-q1b (#939): record each verifier call for this claim with its reasoning
597:            # held SEPARATE from raw_text (the bare verdict/body). This is the verifiers' analogue
598:            # of the generator's reasoning_trace.jsonl.
599:            for record in result.records:
600:                role_call_log.append(
601:                    {
602:                        "claim_id": claim.claim_id,
603:                        "role": record.role,
604:                        "model_slug": record.model_slug,
605:                        "served_model": record.served_model,
606:                        "raw_text": record.raw_text,
607:                        "reasoning": record.reasoning,
608:                    }
609:                )
610:
611:            # I-run11-001 (#1042): INCREMENTALLY persist the role-call log after EACH claim is
612:            # reduced (rewrite the whole file in claim order — small, fine) so a mid-run hang is
613:            # monitorable on disk instead of the log only landing after the full loop. The final
614:            # write below is kept (idempotent: it rewrites the same complete content).
615:            _write_role_call_log(role_calls_path, role_call_log)
616:
617:            # Coverage credit ONLY on a VERIFIED final verdict, against the CANONICAL required
618:            # ids this claim covers — a dropped/UNSUPPORTED claim adds nothing (denominator is
619:            # the fixed required set, so this can only ever lower the achieved fraction).
620:            if result.final_verdict == _VERDICT_VERIFIED:
621:                internal_ledger.covered_element_ids.update(claim.covered_element_ids)
622:
623:            # Snowball KG: persist EVERY outcome (audit); only VERIFIED rows are reusable
624:            # (anti-poisoning is enforced inside the store). role_verdicts records the raw
625:            # Mirror/Sentinel/Judge signals for provenance. KG writes stay PARENT-only (single
626:            # SQLite connection) — never inside a worker (Codex Path-B risk #2).
627:            kg_store.write_claim(
628:                claim_text=claim.claim_text,
629:                claim_id=claim.claim_id,
630:                verdict=result.final_verdict,
631:                role_verdicts={
632:                    "mirror_classification": (
633:                        result.mirror_result.classification
634:                        if result.mirror_result is not None
635:                        else None
636:                    ),
637:                    "sentinel_verdict": (
638:                        result.sentinel_result.verdict.value
639:                        if result.sentinel_result is not None
640:                        else None
641:                    ),
642:                    "raw_judge_verdict": result.raw_judge_verdict,
643:                    "final_verdict": result.final_verdict,
644:                },
645:                timestamp=timestamp,
646:            )
647:        kg_path = Path(kg_store.db_path)
648:    finally:
649:        kg_store.close()
650:
651:    # I-meta-002-q1b (#939): persist the per-role-call reasoning log next to the run — one JSON
652:    # object per line, `reasoning` in its own field, NEVER mixed into the verdict. Reviewable
653:    # line-by-line alongside the generator's reasoning_trace.jsonl. (Kept as the final write even
654:    # though I-run11-001 also writes incrementally above — idempotent same-content rewrite.)
655:    _write_role_call_log(role_calls_path, role_call_log)
656:
657:    # The D8 threshold is loaded from config (LAW VI, pure file read — no network).
658:    config = load_d8_policy_config(d8_config_path)
659:
660:    decision: ReleaseDecision = apply_d8_release_policy(
661:        d8_rows,
662:        required_s0_categories=required_s0_categories,
663:        coverage_ledger=internal_ledger,
664:        coverage_threshold=config.coverage_threshold,
665:        rewrite_already_attempted=rewrite_already_attempted,
666:    )
667:
668:    # I-perm-001 (#1195) slice 2: compute the always-release-aware outcome HERE, where the
669:    # required-S0 set + the per-claim verdicts are natively available. `compute_release_outcome`
670:    # reads PG_ALWAYS_RELEASE (default OFF -> released == decision.release_allowed, byte-identical).
671:    _final = final_verdicts or {}
672:    _zero_verified = not any(v == "VERIFIED" for v in _final.values())
673:    # zero_usable_evidence = the NATIVE evidence signal (Codex slice-2 P1): no claim cites ANY
674:    # evidence document. `not final_verdicts` (no claims) was too weak — a claims-present-but-
675:    # all-unsupported run with no cited evidence must still zero-grounding hard-block. Mirrors the
676:    # replay harness's audit_map evidence_ids signal.
677:    _zero_usable_evidence = not any((c.evidence_documents or []) for c in claims)
678:    _missing_s0 = {
679:        reason[len("d8_s0_must_cover_missing:"):]
680:        for reason in decision.held_reasons
681:        if reason.startswith("d8_s0_must_cover_missing:")
682:    }
683:    _required_s0 = set(required_s0_categories)
684:    _safety_floor_insufficient = bool(_required_s0) and _required_s0 <= _missing_s0
685:    release_outcome = compute_release_outcome(
686:        decision,
687:        zero_verified=_zero_verified,
688:        zero_usable_evidence=_zero_usable_evidence,
689:        safety_floor_insufficient=_safety_floor_insufficient,
690:        coverage_fraction=internal_ledger.fraction(),
691:    )
692:
693:    return FourRoleEvaluationResult(
694:        release_allowed=decision.release_allowed,
695:        held_reasons=decision.held_reasons,
696:        gaps=decision.gaps,
697:        final_verdicts=final_verdicts,
698:        records=all_records,
699:        coverage_fraction=internal_ledger.fraction(),
700:        fabricated_occurrence_latched=decision.fabricated_occurrence_latched,
701:        needs_rewrite=decision.needs_rewrite,
702:        kg_path=kg_path,
703:        release_outcome=release_outcome,
704:    )

741:    heartbeat_claims_cb=None,

743:    """Resolve the 4-role inputs (builder WINS), run the SINGLE binding D8 gate, persist audit.
744:
745:    This is the seam core extracted so BOTH the guarded `run_one_query` branch and the offline
746:    seam test exercise the SAME code (no copy-paste of the override logic). Precedence (Codex
747:    M3 P2 #1): if `four_role_input_builder` is provided it WINS — the SEAM calls it AFTER
748:    generation with the run-local objects (`multi`, `template`, `slug`, `domain`, `ev_pool`) so
749:    it PRODUCES the inputs+audit bundle from the finished report, and the SEAM writes
750:    `bundle.audit_map` to `run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_AUDIT_FILENAME` (json, sorted keys) so every
751:    claim_id is traceable alongside the run. Otherwise a directly-supplied static
752:    `four_role_inputs` is used as-is (unit/static path; it carries no audit_map, so nothing is
753:    written). If BOTH are None the branch fails closed (the sweep never synthesizes inputs).
754:

756:    because `multi`/`ev_pool` only exist inside `run_one_query` after generation; the builder
757:    cannot have closed over them when the caller constructed it. Duck-typed `object` here so this
758:    seam never imports the generator's `MultiSectionResult` (LAW VII CLI isolation).
759:

761:    """

783:            heartbeat_claims_cb=heartbeat_claims_cb,
784:        )
785:        # The SEAM (not the builder) persists the per-claim audit map alongside the run.
786:        (run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_AUDIT_FILENAME).write_text(
787:            json.dumps(bundle.audit_map, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n",
788:            encoding="utf-8",
789:        )
790:        return result
791:
792:    if four_role_inputs is None:
793:        raise ValueError(

795:            "neither a four_role_input_builder nor static four_role_inputs was supplied; the "
796:            "sweep does not synthesize them (fail-closed)."
797:        )
798:
799:    # Static path (no builder): use the caller-supplied inputs as-is (no audit_map to persist).
800:    return run_four_role_evaluation(
801:        transport,
802:        claims=four_role_inputs.claims,
803:        run_dir=run_dir,
804:        timestamp=timestamp,

27:a full resolved URL and thus fails closed (P2 #4). The URL pair is ASYMMETRIC: entity

46:# --- severity vocabulary (mirrors release_policy / d8 config; never an Enum) -------------
47:_SEVERITY_S0 = "S0"
48:_SEVERITY_S1 = "S1"
49:_SEVERITY_S2 = "S2"
50:_SEVERITY_S3 = "S3"
51:_VALID_SEVERITIES = (_SEVERITY_S0, _SEVERITY_S1, _SEVERITY_S2, _SEVERITY_S3)
52:# Rank used to pick the MAX severity over the entities a claim covers (S0 strongest).
53:_SEVERITY_RANK = {_SEVERITY_S0: 3, _SEVERITY_S1: 2, _SEVERITY_S2: 1, _SEVERITY_S3: 0}
54:# A claim that covers no required entity is observe-only (S3) — never gates / never latches.
55:_DEFAULT_OBSERVE_ONLY_SEVERITY = _SEVERITY_S3
56:
57:# --- native contract keys (read from the scope template ONLY) ----------------------------
58:_KEY_REPORT_CONTRACT = "per_query_report_contract"
59:_KEY_REQUIRED_ENTITIES = "required_entities"
60:_KEY_ENTITY_ID = "id"
61:_KEY_ENTITY_SEVERITY = "severity"
62:_KEY_ENTITY_S0_CATEGORY = "s0_category"
63:_KEY_ENTITY_CONTENT_REQS = "coverage_content_requirements"
64:# Canonical-identifier match pairs: (entity_key, record_key). The native scope entity
65:# declares its canonical URL under `url_pattern` (clinical.yaml regulatory entities) and its
66:# trial identity under `doi`/`pmid`; the resolved evidence RECORD carries the served `url`
67:# (M3b normalizes `source_url` -> `url`) plus `doi`/`pmid`. The match is EXACT EQUALITY per
68:# pair (P2 #4): a broad/fragment `url_pattern` can never `==` a full resolved URL, so it
69:# fails closed. The pairing is intentionally ASYMMETRIC (entity `url_pattern` vs record `url`).
70:_CANONICAL_MATCH_PAIRS = (("doi", "doi"), ("pmid", "pmid"), ("url_pattern", "url"))
71:# The entity-side keys the builder recognizes as a canonical identifier (used by the
72:# fail-loud "entity must declare a recognized identifier" guard).
73:_ENTITY_CANONICAL_KEYS = tuple(entity_key for entity_key, _ in _CANONICAL_MATCH_PAIRS)
74:_RECORD_TEXT_KEY = "text"
75:
76:_WHITESPACE_RE = re.compile(r"\s+")
77:_CLAIM_HASH_HEX_LEN = 8
78:
79:# --- evidence-record normalization (M3b; LOAD-BEARING, deterministic, NO network) ---------
80:# The raw evidence_pool.json row carries `source_url` + the evidence text under `direct_quote`
81:# (the field strict_verify's ProvenanceToken spans index into — see provenance_generator.py)
82:# with `statement` as a fallback. It carries NO doi/pmid/url keys. M3b NORMALIZES each row into
83:# the builder's `{text, doi?, pmid?, url?}` record contract so coverage can match the entity's
84:# canonical identifiers. EXACT-equality coverage (P2 #4) means the DOI/PMID must be the bare
85:# canonical token (e.g. `10.1056/NEJMoa2107519`, `34170647`) — never a URL-embedded fragment.
86:_RAW_TEXT_KEYS = ("direct_quote", "statement", "text")
87:_RAW_SOURCE_URL_KEYS = ("source_url", "url")
88:# Deterministic DOI: the canonical `10.<registrant>/<suffix>` form (CrossRef pattern).
89:_DOI_RE = re.compile(r"10\.\d{4,9}/[-._;()/:A-Za-z0-9]+")
90:# Publisher URL path-suffixes appended AFTER the DOI in a landing-page URL (e.g.
91:# frontiersin.org/.../10.3389/fphar.2022.1016639/full). Trimmed so the extracted DOI is the
92:# bare canonical token that EXACTLY equals the entity's `doi` (P2 #4). Order matters: longest
93:# first. Trailing punctuation (a `.` or `;` lifted from prose) is also stripped.
94:_DOI_URL_SUFFIXES = ("/full", "/abstract", "/pdf", "/meta", "/html", "/epdf")
95:_DOI_TRAILING_PUNCT = ".,;)"
96:# Deterministic PMID: a PubMed URL path id (`pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/<id>` or `/pubmed/<id>`)
97:# or an explicit `PMID: <id>` token. Bare numeric so it `==` the entity's `pmid` (int -> str).
98:_PMID_URL_RE = re.compile(r"(?:ncbi\.nlm\.nih\.gov/(?:pubmed|m/pubmed)?/?|/pubmed/)(\d+)")
99:_PMID_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\bPMID:?\s*(\d+)", re.IGNORECASE)

105:
106:    The builder does NO file I/O — it RETURNS this bundle. M3b writes
107:    `four_role_claim_audit.json` from `audit_map` next to the run. `inputs` is fed
108:    verbatim to `run_four_role_evaluation`.
109:    """

115:def _normalize_sentence(sentence: str) -> str:
116:    """Lowercase + collapse whitespace (the basis for the deterministic claim_id hash)."""
117:    return _WHITESPACE_RE.sub(" ", sentence.lower()).strip()
118:
119:
120:def _row_text(row: Mapping[str, Any]) -> str:
121:    """The evidence text the strict_verify spans were validated against (first non-empty).
122:
123:    Prefers `direct_quote` (the field ProvenanceToken char-spans index into), then `statement`,
124:    then `text`. Empty text is NOT raised here — the builder's `_resolve_evidence` fails closed
125:    on empty text at claim-resolution time (so an evidence row never cited stays harmless).
126:    """
127:    for key in _RAW_TEXT_KEYS:
128:        value = row.get(key)
129:        if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip():
130:            return value.strip()
131:    return ""
132:
133:
134:def _row_source_url(row: Mapping[str, Any]) -> str:
135:    """The record's full canonical source URL (verbatim), from `source_url` then `url`."""
136:    for key in _RAW_SOURCE_URL_KEYS:
137:        value = row.get(key)
138:        if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip():
139:            return value.strip()
140:    return ""
141:
142:
143:def _extract_doi(*texts: str) -> str | None:
144:    """Deterministic bare-DOI extraction (`10.<reg>/<suffix>`) from the given strings.
145:
146:    The greedy DOI body can absorb a publisher landing-page suffix (`/full`, `/pdf`, ...) or a
147:    trailing punctuation mark lifted from prose. Both are deterministically trimmed so the
148:    returned DOI is the bare canonical token that EXACTLY equals the entity's `doi` (P2 #4);
149:    coverage stays fail-closed (a mis-trim simply fails to match — never over-credits).
150:    """
151:    for text in texts:
152:        if not text:
153:            continue
154:        match = _DOI_RE.search(text)
155:        if not match:
156:            continue
157:        doi = match.group(0)
158:        for suffix in _DOI_URL_SUFFIXES:
159:            if doi.endswith(suffix):
160:                doi = doi[: -len(suffix)]
161:                break
162:        return doi.rstrip(_DOI_TRAILING_PUNCT)
163:    return None
164:
165:
166:def _extract_pmid(*texts: str) -> str | None:
167:    """Deterministic bare-PMID extraction from a PubMed URL or an explicit `PMID:` token."""
168:    for text in texts:
169:        if not text:
170:            continue
171:        url_match = _PMID_URL_RE.search(text)
172:        if url_match:
173:            return url_match.group(1)
174:        token_match = _PMID_TOKEN_RE.search(text)
175:        if token_match:
176:            return token_match.group(1)
177:    return None
178:
179:
180:def normalize_evidence_pool_lookup(
181:    ev_pool: Mapping[str, Mapping[str, Any]],
182:) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
183:    """Build the builder's `evidence_id -> {text, doi?, pmid?, url?}` lookup from a raw pool.
184:
185:    DETERMINISTIC, NO NETWORK (M3b). Keys are preserved verbatim so they match the
186:    ProvenanceToken.evidence_id space (the same `ev_pool` keyspace the generator used). For each
187:    row: `url` = the record's `source_url` (full canonical URL, verbatim); `doi` = a bare DOI
188:    extracted by regex from the source_url then text (absent if none); `pmid` = a bare PMID from
189:    a PubMed URL or explicit token (absent if none); `text` = the evidence text strict_verify
190:    validated against (`direct_quote`/`statement`/`text`). Optional identifiers are only added
191:    when present so an absent identifier is genuinely absent (the builder treats `None`/`""` as
192:    no-match, fail-closed). Never reads `outputs/dr_benchmark/`.
193:    """
194:    lookup: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
195:    for evidence_id, row in ev_pool.items():
196:        if not isinstance(row, Mapping):
197:            raise ValueError(
198:                f"normalize_evidence_pool_lookup: evidence row {evidence_id!r} is not a mapping "
199:                f"({type(row).__name__}); cannot normalize a non-record (fail-closed)."
200:            )
201:        text = _row_text(row)
202:        url = _row_source_url(row)
203:        record: dict[str, Any] = {_RECORD_TEXT_KEY: text}
204:        if url:
205:            record["url"] = url
206:        doi = _extract_doi(url, text)
207:        if doi is not None:
208:            record["doi"] = doi
209:        pmid = _extract_pmid(url, text)
210:        if pmid is not None:
211:            record["pmid"] = pmid
212:        lookup[evidence_id] = record
213:    return lookup

216:def load_required_entities(template: dict, slug: str) -> list[dict]:
217:    """Return the NATIVE required entities for `slug`; fail closed if absent/empty.
218:
219:    The native denominator MUST exist — a missing contract or empty entity list raises
220:    (never a vacuous empty-denominator pass).
221:    """
222:    contracts = template.get(_KEY_REPORT_CONTRACT)
223:    if not isinstance(contracts, dict) or slug not in contracts:
224:        raise ValueError(
225:            f"load_required_entities: no {_KEY_REPORT_CONTRACT}[{slug!r}] in the scope "
226:            f"template; the native required-element denominator must exist (fail-closed)."
227:        )
228:    entities = contracts[slug].get(_KEY_REQUIRED_ENTITIES)
229:    if not isinstance(entities, list) or not entities:
230:        raise ValueError(
231:            f"load_required_entities: {_KEY_REPORT_CONTRACT}[{slug!r}].{_KEY_REQUIRED_ENTITIES} "
232:            f"is missing or empty; cannot build a coverage denominator (fail-closed)."
233:        )
234:    return entities

237:def validate_entity_severity(
238:    entity: dict, d8_config: D8PolicyConfig
239:) -> tuple[str, str | None]:
240:    """§7.E schema-validator (FAIL CLOSED — Codex P1 iter1). Never defaults to S3.
241:
242:    Returns (severity, s0_category_or_None). Raises on a missing/invalid severity, an entity
243:    that declares NO builder-recognized canonical identifier (doi/pmid/url_pattern — else it
244:    would be silently uncoverable), an S0 entity without a valid `s0_category` in the D8
245:    must-cover vocabulary, or an S0 entity without a non-empty `coverage_content_requirements`.
246:    """
247:    severity = entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_SEVERITY)
248:    if severity not in _VALID_SEVERITIES:
249:        raise ValueError(
250:            f"validate_entity_severity: entity {entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_ID)!r} has "
251:            f"severity={severity!r}; must be one of {_VALID_SEVERITIES} (NEVER default S3)."
252:        )
253:    # Every required entity MUST declare at least one canonical identifier the builder can
254:    # match on (doi / pmid / url_pattern). An identifier-less entity is permanently
255:    # uncoverable — make that a LOUD config error rather than a silent coverage loss.
256:    if not any(entity.get(key) for key in _ENTITY_CANONICAL_KEYS):
257:        raise ValueError(
258:            f"validate_entity_severity: entity {entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_ID)!r} declares no "
259:            f"canonical identifier among {_ENTITY_CANONICAL_KEYS}; it would be permanently "
260:            f"uncoverable (fail-closed)."
261:        )
262:    if severity != _SEVERITY_S0:
263:        return severity, None
264:
265:    s0_category = entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_S0_CATEGORY)
266:    if not s0_category or s0_category not in d8_config.s0_must_cover_categories:
267:        raise ValueError(
268:            f"validate_entity_severity: S0 entity {entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_ID)!r} declares "
269:            f"s0_category={s0_category!r} which is missing or not in the D8 must-cover "
270:            f"vocabulary {tuple(d8_config.s0_must_cover_categories)} (fail-closed)."
271:        )
272:    content_reqs = entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_CONTENT_REQS)
273:    if not isinstance(content_reqs, list) or not content_reqs:
274:        raise ValueError(
275:            f"validate_entity_severity: S0 entity {entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_ID)!r} has no "
276:            f"non-empty {_KEY_ENTITY_CONTENT_REQS}; an S0 safety category requires "
277:            f"deterministic content tokens to credit coverage (fail-closed)."
278:        )
279:    # Every requirement token must be a NON-BLANK string. A list like [''] or ['   '] or
280:    # [123] would otherwise pass the truthy-list check above and then let a bare canonical
281:    # citation wrongly earn S0 credit (Codex P1: never validate an S0 entity whose content
282:    # requirements are empty/blank/non-string after .strip()).
283:    for token in content_reqs:
284:        if not isinstance(token, str) or not token.strip():
285:            raise ValueError(
286:                f"validate_entity_severity: S0 entity {entity.get(_KEY_ENTITY_ID)!r} has a "
287:                f"{_KEY_ENTITY_CONTENT_REQS} element {token!r} that is not a non-blank string; "
288:                f"every S0 content requirement must be a real deterministic token (fail-closed)."
289:            )
290:    return severity, s0_category

292:
293:def _entity_canonical_match(entity: dict, record: Mapping[str, Any]) -> bool:
294:    """EXACT canonical-identifier match (P2 #4): DOI / PMID / full canonical URL.
295:
296:    Equality per (entity_key, record_key) pair only — never substring. The URL pair compares
297:    the entity's `url_pattern` against the record's resolved `url`; a broad `url_pattern`
298:    FRAGMENT can never equal a full resolved URL, so it fails closed.
299:    """
300:    for entity_key, record_key in _CANONICAL_MATCH_PAIRS:
301:        entity_value = entity.get(entity_key)
302:        if entity_value in (None, ""):
303:            continue
304:        record_value = record.get(record_key)
305:        if record_value in (None, ""):
306:            continue
307:        if str(entity_value).strip() == str(record_value).strip():
308:            return True
309:    return False
